class="reviewTitle_1qq1j"><span>Great controller with very unique haptic features</span></div><div class="reviewerInfo_twVGf"><span class="author_20vgR">Reviewed by <span><span><span>Adam</span></span></span></span> <span class="locationAndTime_3MA78" data-automation="rating-date" data-date="2020-11-18T21:02:48">- November 18, 2020</span></div><div class="reviewContent_XCspv"><p><span>At a first glance, this controller looks like a pretty standard offering for a game console. It has a nicer weight to it and seems to have a better build quality compared to the DS4, but otherwise it appears relatively unchanged. However, my opinion changed instantly after trying out the controller in game. Astro's Play Room was a fantastic demo for what the haptic features of the controller are capable of. Zipping up a zipper using the touch pad and actually 'feeling' the zipper go up was something I didn't think was achievable using haptic feedback. In an FPS (Borderlands 3) I could feel the difference in trigger pulls between a shot gun and an SMG. It took more force to pull the trigger on the shot gun, and the haptic feedback felt like the gun actually kicked back. This will be a new standard going forward in video game controller design.</span></p></div><div class="recommendedIconsContainer_3sOAY"><svg focusable="false" viewBox="0 0 34 34" class="black_3d_RE icon_q2ZYd recommendedIcons_1e-hN"><path class="cls-1" d="M18,2.1A15.9,15.9,0,1,0,33.9,18,15.91,15.91,0,0,0,18,2.1Zm0,30A14.1,14.1,0,1,1,32.1,18,14.12,14.12,0,0,1,18,32.1Z"></path><path class="cls-1" d="M27.11,19.22a.9.9,0,0,0-1.23.33,9.1,9.1,0,0,1-15.76,0,.9.9,0,0,0-1.56.9,10.9,10.9,0,0,0,18.88,0A.9.9,0,0,0,27.11,19.22Z"></path><circle class="cls-1" cx="12" cy="13" r="2"></circle><circle class="cls-1" cx="24" cy="13" r="2"></circle></svg></div><div class="friendRecommendationTextContainer_1Cqdj"><span class="friendRecommendationOption_vxQ_h">Yes, </span><span>I would recommend this to a friend.</span></div><div data-automation="helpfulness-feedback-container" class="reviewFeedbackContainer_2ulTr"><div data-automation="helpful-button-container" class="reviewFeedbackInnerContainer_tSrG5"><svg focusable="false" viewBox="0 0 34 34" class="blue_2GwtG icon_q2ZYd feedbackIcon_N7x5r"><path d="M28.76,13.09h-6a.31.31,0,0,1-.3-.3V7.15a3,3,0,0,0-3-3A3.39,3.39,
